<script>
window.fpPromise = import('https://openfpcdn.io/fingerprintjs/v4')
.then(FingerprintJS => FingerprintJS.load())
window.fpPromise
.then(fp => fp.get())
.then(result => {
	const visitorId = result.visitorId
	localStorage.setItem('visitorId', visitorId);
})

function getVisitorId() {
	return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
		if (localStorage.getItem('visitorId')) {
			resolve(localStorage.getItem('visitorId'));
		} else {
			window.fpPromise
			.then(fp => fp.get())
			.then(result => {
				const visitorId = result.visitorId
				localStorage.setItem('visitorId', visitorId);
				resolve(visitorId);
			})
		}
	});
}

function waitForAnalyticsPermission() {
	return new Promise((resolve) => {
		function checkPermission() {
			console.log('check AnalyticsPermission', window.adskGdprAnalytics)
			if (window.location.hostname === 'wordpress2.aec.loc' || window.location.hostname === 'wp.aecpartners.of1.weborchestra.org') {
				resolve(true);
			} else {
				if (
					window.adskGdpr && window.adskGdpr.gdprCheck === true && (window.adskGdprAnalytics === true || window.adskGdprAnalytics === false)
					|| window.adskGdprAnalytics === true
				) {
					resolve(window.adskGdprAnalytics);
				} else {
					setTimeout(checkPermission, 230);
				}
			}
		}

		checkPermission();
	});
}

function aec_ga(event_type, type_event, category, action, label, value) {
	// console.log(window.adskGdpr, window.adskGdpr && window.adskGdpr.gdprCheck !== true)
	// if (window.adskGdpr && window.adskGdpr.gdprCheck !== true) {
	// 	typeof value['hitCallback'];
	// }
	if (window.adskGdpr && window.adskGdpr.gdprCheck !== true && window.adskGdprAnalytics !== true) {
		if (value && typeof value['hitCallback'] !== 'undefined') {
			setTimeout(() => {
				value['hitCallback']();
			}, 250);
		}
	}

	waitForAnalyticsPermission().then((res) => {
		if (res == true) {
			getVisitorId().then(visitorId => {
				jQuery.ajax({
					"url" : "https://aecpartners.autodesk.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php?action=aec_analytics",
					"data": {
						category: category,
						label: btoa(label),
						event_action: action,
						value: value,
						visitor_id: visitorId,
					}
				} ).done(function (a, b, c){});
			})
		} else {
			if (typeof value['hitCallback'] !== 'undefined') {
				value['hitCallback']();
			}
		}
	})


}

jQuery(document).ready(() => {
	if (jQuery(".aec-tiles-container").length > 0) {
		var pageUid = JSON.stringify({
			lang: "en",
			id: 0,
			uid: 'TILES',
			url: window.location.href,
		});
		aec_ga('aec.send', 'event', 'page', 'view', pageUid);
	} else {
		var pageUid = JSON.stringify({
			lang: "en",
			id: jQuery(".aec-vendor-details").data("id"),
			uid: jQuery(".aec-vendor-details").data("uid"),
			url: window.location.href,
		});
		aec_ga('aec.send', 'event', 'page', 'view', pageUid);
	}

	jQuery(".aec-tiles-container").click(function (e){
		jQuery(e.target).parents("a.aec-vendor-tile").each(function (idx, el){
			e.preventDefault();

			aec_ga('aec.send', 'event', 'product_tile', 'click', jQuery(el).data("id")+"-"+jQuery(el).data("uid"), {
				hitCallback : function (){
					location.href = jQuery(el).attr("href");
				}
			});
		})
	})

	jQuery(".aec-category-filter").change(function (e){
		aec_ga('aec.send', 'event', 'search', 'category', jQuery(".aec-category-filter").val()+"-"+jQuery("select.aec-category-filter option:selected").text());
	});

	jQuery(document).bind("aec.search", function (e, text){
		aec_ga('aec.send', 'event', 'search', 'text', jQuery(".aec-category-filter").val()+"-"+jQuery("select.aec-category-filter option:selected").text());
	})
});
</script>
